DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ITEMVARIANTDOCUMENT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS TAGDOCUMENT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS SECTIONDOCUMENT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS UNITDOCUMENT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PROJECTDOCUMENT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PROCUREMENT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ITEM
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS TAG
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS SECTION
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS UNIT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ITEMVARIANT
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS PROJECT

GO 

IF EXISTS(
SELECT * 
FROM sys.objects
WHERE TYPE = 'P' AND NAME = 'sp_ReadTagFromDatabase')
DROP PROCEDURE sp_ReadTagFromDatabase

GO 
IF EXISTS(
SELECT * 
FROM sys.objects
WHERE TYPE = 'P' AND NAME = 'sp_ReadProjectFromDatabase')
DROP PROCEDURE sp_ReadProjectFromDatabase

GO

IF EXISTS(
SELECT * 
FROM sys.objects
WHERE TYPE = 'P' AND NAME = 'sp_ReadUnitFromDatabase')
DROP PROCEDURE sp_ReadUnitFromDatabase 

GO 

IF EXISTS(
SELECT * 
FROM sys.objects
WHERE TYPE = 'P' AND NAME = 'sp_ReadItemFromDatabase')
DROP PROCEDURE sp_ReadItemFromDatabase 

GO

IF EXISTS(
SELECT * 
FROM sys.objects
WHERE TYPE = 'P' AND NAME = 'sp_ReadSectionFromDatabase')
DROP PROCEDURE sp_ReadSectionFromDatabase 

GO

IF EXISTS(
SELECT * 
FROM sys.objects 
WHERE TYPE = 'P' AND NAME = 'sp_InsertNewSerialNumberIntoItem')
DROP PROCEDURE sp_InsertNewSerialNumberIntoItem

GO

CREATE TABLE PROJECT( 
ProjectNumber NVARCHAR(50),
ProjectDescription NVARCHAR(100)
CONSTRAINT Project_PK PRIMARY KEY (ProjectNumber))  

GO 

CREATE TABLE ITEMVARIANT(
ItemVariantID INT NOT NULL IDENTITY (1,1),
ItemNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
ItemDescription NVARCHAR(100), 
CONSTRAINT ITEMVARIANT_PK PRIMARY KEY (ItemVariantID)) 

GO 

CREATE TABLE UNIT(
UnitNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
UnitDescription NVARCHAR(50), 
ProjectNumber NVARCHAR(50),
CONSTRAINT UNIT_PK PRIMARY KEY(UnitNumber, ProjectNumber),
CONSTRAINT UNIT_FK FOREIGN KEY(ProjectNumber) 
REFERENCES PROJECT(ProjectNumber)); 

GO 

CREATE TABLE SECTION(
SectionNumber INT, 
OldSectionNumber INT, 
Title NVARCHAR(100),
UnitNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
ProjectNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
CONSTRAINT SECTION_PK PRIMARY KEY (SectionNumber, UnitNumber, ProjectNumber), 
CONSTRAINT SECTION_FK_SECTION_UNIT FOREIGN KEY(UnitNumber,ProjectNumber) 
REFERENCES UNIT(UnitNumber,ProjectNumber));

GO

CREATE TABLE TAG(
TagNumber NVARCHAR(50),
UnionTagNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
TagLineNumber INT, 
TagDescription NVARCHAR(100), 
HaffManTag NVARCHAR(50), 
CustomerTag NVARCHAR(50), 
VendorTag NVARCHAR(50),
BelongsTo NVARCHAR(50),
ProjectNumber NVARCHAR(50),
SectionNumber INT, 
UnitNumber NVARCHAR(50),  

CONSTRAINT TAG_PK PRIMARY KEY (TagNumber, ProjectNumber),
CONSTRAINT TAG_FK_TAG_SECTION FOREIGN KEY(SectionNumber, UnitNumber, ProjectNumber) 
REFERENCES SECTION(SectionNumber, UnitNumber, ProjectNumber)); 

GO 

CREATE TABLE ITEM(
ItemID INT IDENTITY(100,1), 
ItemLineNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
UnitOfMeasure NVARCHAR(20), 
Quantity NVARCHAR(20), 
SerialNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
ItemVariantID INT, 
ProjectNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
TagNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
CONSTRAINT ITEM_PK PRIMARY KEY(ItemId), 
CONSTRAINT ITEM_FK_ITEM_ITEMVARIANT FOREIGN KEY(ItemVariantID) 
REFERENCES ITEMVARIANT(ItemVariantID), 
CONSTRAINT ITEM_FK_ITEM_TAG FOREIGN KEY (TagNumber,ProjectNumber) 
REFERENCES TAG(TagNumber, ProjectNumber)); 


GO 

CREATE TABLE PROCUREMENT(
ProcurementID INT IDENTITY (1,1), 
ProcurementStatus NVARCHAR(20), 
PurchaseOrderNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
ItemID INT NOT NULL, 
CONSTRAINT PROCUREMENT_PK PRIMARY KEY (ProcurementID),
CONSTRAINT PROCUREMENT_FK FOREIGN KEY (ItemID) 
REFERENCES ITEM(ItemID)); 

GO 

CREATE TABLE PROJECTDOCUMENT(
PTitle NVARCHAR(200),
PDocDescription NVARCHAR(100), 
PFile NVARCHAR(200), 
ProjectNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
CONSTRAINT PROJECTDOCUMENT_PK PRIMARY KEY (PTitle),
CONSTRAINT PROJECTDOCUMENT_FK FOREIGN KEY(ProjectNumber) 
REFERENCES PROJECT(ProjectNumber));

GO 

CREATE TABLE UNITDOCUMENT(
UTitle NVARCHAR(200),
UDocDescription NVARCHAR(100), 
UFile NVARCHAR(200), 
ProjectNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
UnitNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
CONSTRAINT UNITDOCUMENT_PK PRIMARY KEY(UTitle),
CONSTRAINT UNITDOCUMENT_FK_UNITDOC_UNIT FOREIGN KEY(UnitNumber, ProjectNumber)
REFERENCES UNIT(UnitNumber,ProjectNumber)); 

GO 

CREATE TABLE SECTIONDOCUMENT(
STitle NVARCHAR(200), 
SDocDescription NVARCHAR(100),
SFile NVARCHAR(200),
ProjectNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
UnitNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
SectionNumber INT,
CONSTRAINT SECTIONDOCUMENT_PK PRIMARY KEY(STitle), 
CONSTRAINT SECTIONDOCUMENT_FK_SECTIONDOC_SECTION FOREIGN KEY(SectionNumber, UnitNumber, ProjectNumber)
REFERENCES SECTION(SectionNumber, UnitNumber, ProjectNumber)); 

GO 

CREATE TABLE TAGDOCUMENT(
TTitle NVARCHAR(200),
TDocDescription NVARCHAR(100),
TFile NVARCHAR(200),
TagNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
ProjectNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
CONSTRAINT TAGDOCUMENT_PK PRIMARY KEY(TTitle), 
CONSTRAINT TAGDOCUMENT_FK FOREIGN KEY(TagNumber, ProjectNumber) 
REFERENCES TAG(TagNumber, ProjectNumber)); 

GO 

CREATE TABLE ITEMVARIANTDOCUMENT(
ITitle NVARCHAR(200), 
IDocDescription NVARCHAR(100),
IFILE NVARCHAR(200), 
ItemVariantID INT NOT NULL,
CONSTRAINT ITEMVARIANTDOCUMENT_PK PRIMARY KEY(ITitle),
CONSTRAINT ITEMVARIANTDOCUMENT_FK FOREIGN KEY(ItemVariantID)
REFERENCES ITEMVARIANT(ItemVariantID));

CREATE PROCEDURE sp_ReadTagFromDatabase
	@projectNum NVARCHAR (50)
AS 
BEGIN
SELECT TG.TagNumber, TG.UnionTagNumber, TG.TagLineNumber, TG.TagDescription, TG.HaffmanTag, TG.CustomerTag, TG.VendorTag, TG.BelongsTo, TG.SectionNumber, 
TGD.TTitle, TGD.TDocDescription, TGD.TFile
FROM TAG TG
INNER JOIN TAGDOCUMENT TGD 
	ON TG.ProjectNumber = TGD.ProjectNumber 
WHERE TG.ProjectNumber = @projectNum
END;

GO

CREATE PROCEDURE sp_ReadProjectFromDatabase
    @projectNum NVARCHAR(50)
AS 
BEGIN
SELECT PR.ProjectNumber, PR.ProjectDescription,
PRD.PTitle, PRD.PDocDescription, PRD.PFile
FROM PROJECT PR
LEFT JOIN PROJECTDOCUMENT PRD ON PR.ProjectNumber = PRD.ProjectNumber
WHERE PR.ProjectNumber = @projectNum
END; 

GO


CREATE PROCEDURE sp_ReadUnitFromDatabase
    @projectNum NVARCHAR(50)
AS
BEGIN
SELECT UN.UnitNumber, UN.UnitDescription,
UND.UTitle, UND.UDocDescription, UND.UFile
FROM UNIT UN
LEFT JOIN UNITDOCUMENT UND ON UN.UnitNumber = UND.UnitNumber
WHERE UN.ProjectNumber = @projectNum
END;

GO


CREATE PROCEDURE sp_ReadItemFromDatabase
    @projectNum NVARCHAR(50)
AS
BEGIN
SELECT IT.ItemVariantID, IT.ItemNumber, IT.ItemDescription, 
IM.ItemID, IM.ProjectNumber, IM.ItemLineNumber, IM.UnitOfMeasure, IM.Quantity, IM.TagNumber, IM.SerialNumber,
PR.ProcurementID, PR.ProcurementStatus, PR.PurchaseOrderNumber,
IMD.ITitle, IMD.IDocDescription, IMD.IFile
FROM ITEMVARIANT IT
LEFT JOIN ITEM IM ON IT.ItemVariantID = IM.ItemVariantID
LEFT JOIN PROCUREMENT PR ON IM.ItemID = PR.ItemID
LEFT JOIN TAG TG ON IM.TagNumber = TG.TagNumber
LEFT JOIN ITEMVARIANTDOCUMENT IMD ON IT.ItemVariantID = IMD.ItemVariantID 
WHERE IM.ProjectNumber = @projectNum
END;

GO


CREATE PROCEDURE sp_ReadSectionFromDatabase
    @projectNum NVARCHAR(50)
AS
BEGIN
SELECT SC.SectionNumber, SC.OldSectionNumber, SC.Title, SC.UnitNumber,
SCD.STitle, SCD.SDocDescription, SCD.SFile   
FROM SECTION SC
LEFT JOIN SECTIONDOCUMENT SCD ON SCD.SectionNumber = SC.SectionNumber
WHERE SC.ProjectNumber = @projectNum
END;

GO 

CREATE PROC sp_InsertNewSerialNumberIntoItem
@newSerialNumber NVARCHAR(50), 
@matchingTagNumber NVARCHAR(50)
AS
BEGIN 
UPDATE ITEM 
SET SerialNumber = @newSerialNumber
WHERE TagNumber = @matchingTagNumber 
END;
